<pictures>None< /pictures>< Review>
I've purchased 2 Quads from Fators and their Sales philosophy was much better than any other dealer within 100 miles.  I'm talking all dealers, ie: Yamaha, Honda, Kawasaki, etc, etc.
After laying out the criteria I wanted in a quad, ie: 4 Stroke, Automatic, 4WD, Low Range, etc, the other dealers told me everything from:  "You don't need 4WD, to "With a honda, you don't need low range".
When I informed the Fators salesman what I wanted, he simply showed me the quads that met that criteria and let the quad sell itself.
No BS about other manufacturers, no sales pitch, no pressure.
Excellent Salesmanship!!
As far as service goes, I recently brought my Suzuki Vinson 500 to them for a carburetor issue.  The mechanics, Joe & Duston were very courteous and listened to everything I had to say regarding what led up to the problem.  They had the problem diagnosed in moments and immediately started to work on it.  4 hours later I was driving off with my quad running as well as it ever had.  They overhauled the carburetor and even installed a prefilter in the fuel line to prevent future issues.  They also performed numerous checks and routine maintenance, all at a very reasonable price. The friendly and personable attitude of the Owner and the Mechanics were refreshing and I left a very happy customer.
Great Job Guys!!   Thank You!</Review>

<Resp>None< /Resp>< Review>
A great place for poke, would want to eat again.
Got delivered for lunch. Visually, the color is diverse and vibrant, and I can immediately smell the freshness I expect from a poke bowl.
As a tuna lover who sears tuna steak at least once a week, I can guarantee the tuna is great here. The fish is very fresh and marinated beautifully in the flavorful sauce, definitely the star of the dish. The rice is decent, not too heavily seasoned, and pairs quite well with the spicy fish.
The only minor problem is that the krab salad is rather tasteless, adding soy sauce helps but maybe add some light mayo with the mix could be better. Another suggestion would be to reduce the amount of the seaweed salad, as its sweetness can be a bit overpowering.
Overall a 8.5-9 out of 10, enjoyed it.<//Review>

<rate>4< /rate><Pictures>None</Pictures><userid>111406581821869219432<//userid><Name>Linnea Gimby< /Name>< Review>
I went in the day of Christmas Eve and was seen promptly. The doctor who saw me diagnosed a chest virus but did prescribe antibiotics and OTC cough syrup. I am visiting from Hawaii and visiting friends so you can understand my misery! I went back to my friends house and curled up in bed and hibernated in their guest room until New Years Eve when I decided I was either dying or I wished I was!

On going back in to the clinic with severe, and obvious, pulmonary distress I was advised to take a seat in the full waiting room. I politely told the desk clerk I was having difficulty breathing and I was informed it was first come first served. After listening to me try to breath (no joke I could NOT breath!) my friend, who had driven me because she didn't trust me to drive as I was, went to the counter and rather coldly told the clerk I could not breathe and I needed to be seen NOW!

I was seen almost immediately after that, lol. The doctor looked at my BP, oxygen levels, and chest sounds (around my coughing fits that left me limp and dizzy) and immediately told me I needed to be seen in the ER and I needed an ambulance and an oxygen bottle. My friend said that was good and she would meet me there. They called the ambulance and stayed with me until they arrived, giving me a breathing treatment while we waited. Turns out I had double pneumonia!

So, to recap, I received excellent service from the doctors and medical personnel. The clerks were polite but rather uncaring on the 2nd visit. Just a recommendation,  if someone says they can't breath BELIEVE them!! Otherwise, I do recommend this location.< /Review>

< Review>
Overall, this is an average laundry.  I found Sunshine Laundry clean, with nice machines, few out of order machines, clean carts with working wheels and casters, average prices, and, well, nothing else.  There is limited seating, no attendant, no restroom, no WiFi, no credit card readers, no vending, small folding tables.</Review>

< review>
Tom and Chris are the absolute best in the business, period! After conducting very thorough research, I spoke with the owners of a few car audio shops that proved to be serious about their work. After meeting with Tom, I realized I found the best place to purchase high quality products from and have extremely professional installation performed. Tom and Chris exceeded my lofty expectations and the system is simply fantastic!

Tom and Chris truly care about their product, their reputation, their tremendously clean installations, but most importantly they genuinely care about their customers.  There is no substitute for very professional, pleasant and knowledgeable people who are extremely honest about their business. Tom and Chris take the time to clarify every single aspect of the system you want to put together and have installed.

There was never a time either of these gentlemen pressured me to upgrade any components or accessories. Through the numerous emails and in-person visits, Tom and I discussed what system options were available to me with the budget I had to work with. When discussing my system, Tom and Chris offered options but always allowed every single system decision to be made by me.  Both of these men are very patient, believe me.

I had an entirely new sound system installed, along with a brand new Viper alarm and LED exterior and interior lighting. A custom box was built for my system and the outcome of that was a very pleasant surprise. Tom took the time to customize the box‚Äôs beauty cover to my taste and even included a logo and a nickname, all on his own doing! He did not have to take the time to add any of those features but he did so because he felt it helped put the finishing touches on an excellent system that was installed beautifully. Even the sound dampening was installed very cleanly and most importantly, very effectively.

Tom and Chris are very detailed when it comes to ensuring the wiring is very neat, very organized, and aesthetically pleasing. They both took the time to be very detailed with the alarm installation and they both ensured I was completely satisfied with the alarm. Chris even programmed the Viper alarm for me, right down the color of the display on the remote. Both Tom and Chris took the time to walk me through the details of what they were doing and had done, step by step, to allow me to see exactly what was transpiring with my car. They even voluntarily stayed after hours to complete work on my car!

It is very obvious that Tom and Chris take great pride in their work and the results shine through. Lastly, they are very honorable men and that is very important. They both told me directly to my face that if anything arises with the system, contact them, bring the car in and they will take care of it. They are an authorized dealer of excellent products such as JL Audio and Kenwood, among many others. They honor warranties on all products they sell and the installation has an excellent warranty as well.

If you are wanting minor installations or upgrades, or are very serious about your car system, bring your car to Street Sound Plus! They also take care of headlights, taillights, back-up cameras‚Ä¶and many other audio and accessory options. Please, do yourself a favor and stop by Street Sound Plus to appreciate what they do in person.

I will take my car, and any other car I may purchase in the future, to Tom and Chris for any and all work they handle because they have proven themselves. Keep in mind that you get what you pay for ladies and gentlemen. If you do something, have it done correctly and with as good a quality product as possible. I will proudly display the Street Sound Plus stickers on my car and will play my system proudly and loudly to prove and deeply appreciate their work.

Thank you very, very much Tom and Chris. You have made my car even more pleasurable to drive and I like the looks and compliments I receive about the awesome system you gentlemen installed.</review>

1568915488139</date>
<Rating>2< /Rating><Review>When you first glance inside the lovely windows and doors of Jane on Fillmore, you're met with some pleasant decor and a bustling vibe full of many guests dining away, an impressive 1st impression that unfortunately ends as soon as you walk through the doors.

Right upon entry, this wave of heat straight out of the sahara desert engulfs every inch of your body, making you feel like a young high school wrestler trapped inside of a steaming hot sauna trying to cut weight for a competition tomorrow.

After peeling off every acceptable layer of clothing possible and navigating my order through heat stroke like conditions (Me - Turkey Club Sandwhich; My GF - Avocado Mash), I eagerly awaited the reprieve I would feel once I finally received the delicious brunch food that I was promised through the many positive reviews online.

Unfortunately, my saga did not contain the Cinderella ending that I so desperately hoped for.  While waiting for my food to be finished, I couldn't help but watch all the hard working chefs bustling meticulously away while preparing every dish inside of their open kitchen next to the dining area.

My curiosity indeed killed the cat (or in this case my appetite), watching them create a standard avocado toast consisted of them pulling out a large industrial sized tub of guac that looked like it was purchased from costco, slathering an ungodly amount onto multiple pieces of toast, followed by pre-made already peeled hard boiled eggs also from a tub.  It felt like if McDonald's ever served avocado toast, this would be the conveyor belt method that they would enforce, hardly the expected amount of personalization or individually cut avocado from actual avocados that a $9  price tag should warrant.

Our fears were confirmed when we actually started consuming our food. The egg and guac mash were indeed cold and bland as expected.  My turkey club sandwich was PACKED with 2 small slices of turkey and tasted no better than the sandwiches that anyone could make from the comfort of their own home.

The only saving grace was the magnificent and diverse staff/chefs, who were nice, social, efficient, and must all have some type of reptile blood inside of them to be able to withstand the constant amount of ubiquitous heat on a daily basis.  Props to you guys.< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics><Resp>None< /Resp>< gmapID>

<user>103379264202553362035</user>< username>
Johnny Wang</username>
<Time>1465164099819<//Time><rate>3</rate>< text>
I could have sworn I wrote a review for this months ago, especially having dropped in at least three times by now! In any case, despite all the visits, I've only ever come in to try their pastries, and none of their hot foods. By now, I've had two of their coffee cakes, one of their regular cakes, one of their cookies, and most recently, their scones.

And, honestly? Not all that impressed. Good bakery items, but nothing phenomenal. Their coffee cakes are much tastier than their regular cakes, and their scones are pretty solid too, but you can also find better of the various individual items elsewhere in the city.

***Accessibility Info***

Venue - Jane is a pretty compact venue, with some limited (but accessible) two tops up front, higher (and less accessible) bar height two tops towards the side, and a second floor with some other sort of seating. The ordering counter and the bar two tops end up forming a slightly narrow corridor, that's somewhat difficult to navigate when the place is packed (which is most of the time), but nothing a couple "pardon me"s can't fix. As for ordering itself, I recall the counter being a tad on the high side, which makes it a little harder to see all the pastries they have on display.

Bathroom - No comment because I didn't try them.< /text>

I ordered a black rice porridge which used Goji  berries and chia seeds, both thrown dry on top, instead of being rehydrated as they should, making me think they care more about fashionable ingredients than the way to employ them.

Overall it was good, but there is room for improvement.< /Text>

<UserId.>110002851130159004745</UserId.>< Review>
It's debatable what's Jane's "other" location: the one on Larkin or my to-go spot, the Fillmore Jane's. What's not debatable: you'll get quality coffee, delicious food, all in a lively PacHeights setting. With San Francisco prices. Salad = $9, Banana bread = $3, Chai Latte = $4.

Well, you'll forget about what you just paid once you take a sip of their home-made Chai, or munch on their fresh and tasty granola.

Very very busy, and it'll be hard to find seating any time of day. But: busy for a reason.<//Review>

I was sorely disappointed because there was a strong acidic note that left a sour after taste. If you want Stumptown, get the bottled cold brewed coffee.

I ordered the coffee cake with raspberries. It‚Äôs exactly what you expect when you pick up a coffee cake at CostCo ‚Äì a bar above decent. I‚Äôm not shitting on CostCo‚Äôs baked goods, I‚Äôm just saying that Jane‚Äôs isn‚Äôt something to rave about.

I also ordered the tuna melt. It came with yellow cheddar, tomatoes, and while the tuna had a nice peppery bite, but there was too much mayo. I hate it when watery mayo seeps through the delicious buttery toasted bread and makes it soggy. Other than that, it was decent.< /text>
